-- --------------------------------------------------------

-- 
-- Table structure for table `event`
-- 

CREATE TABLE `event` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `eventTitle` text NOT NULL,
  `cityId` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  `venueName` text NOT NULL,
  `address` text NOT NULL,
  `state` char(2) NOT NULL default '',
  `zip` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  `flyerURL` text NOT NULL,
  `date` datetime NOT NULL default '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  `time` varchar(100) NOT NULL default '',
  `message` text NOT NULL,
  `guestListURL` text NOT NULL,
  `submitted` timestamp NOT NULL default CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `hostName` varchar(250) NOT NULL default '',
  `hostEmail` varchar(250) NOT NULL default '',
  `hostPassword` varchar(100) NOT NULL default '',
  `startDate` date NOT NULL default '0000-00-00',
  `endDate` date NOT NULL default '0000-00-00',
  `weekDay` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  `IsActive` tinyint(1) NOT NULL default '0',
  `webUserId` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=717 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=717 ;

-- 
-- Table structure for table `host`
-- 

CREATE TABLE `host` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `name` text NOT NULL,
  `email` text NOT NULL,
  `website` varchar(250) NOT NULL default '',
  `imgURL` text NOT NULL,
  `text` text NOT NULL,
  `startDate` date NOT NULL default '0000-00-00',
  `endDate` date NOT NULL default '0000-00-00',
  `prevHostId` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=3 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=3 ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

-- 
-- Table structure for table `venue`
-- 

CREATE TABLE `venue` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `name` text NOT NULL,
  `address` text NOT NULL,
  `cityId` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  `imgURL` text NOT NULL,
  `text` text NOT NULL,
  `website` text NOT NULL,
  `IsInternational` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=82 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=82 ;

-- 
-- Table structure for table `venueReview`
-- 

CREATE TABLE `venueReview` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `venueId` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  `webUserId` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  `rating` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  `review` text NOT NULL,
  `date` timestamp NOT NULL default CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `approved` tinyint(1) NOT NULL default '0',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=14 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=14 ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

-- 
-- Table structure for table `webUser`
-- 

CREATE TABLE `webUser` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `firstName` varchar(100) NOT NULL default '',
  `lastName` varchar(100) NOT NULL default '',
  `email` varchar(100) NOT NULL default '',
  `password` varchar(100) NOT NULL default '',
  `cityId` int(11) NOT NULL default '0',
  `isActive` tinyint(1) NOT NULL default '0',
  `confirmationCode` varchar(100) NOT NULL default '',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=14 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=14 ;
